class=\"infobox-header wiki-backgroundcolor-light\">Upcoming Matches</div></div></div></div>\n<p><b>RLCS 2021-22 </b> is the second <a href=\"/rocketleague/RLCS\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"RLCS\">RLCS</a> season in 2021, crossing over into 2022. This season introduces the most major changes to the RLCS system yet with more regions and an updated format. 3 splits - Fall, Winter, Spring - each have 3 regional events leading into an international major. Within all these events, each team collects points that will determine whether they will qualify for the World Championship or World Championship Wildcard.\n</p><p>The <b>RLCS 2021-22 World Championship</b> will take place in Fort Worth, United States at the <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" class=\"external text\" href=\"https://dickiesarena.com/\">Dickies Arena</a>.\n</p>\n<div id=\"toc\" class=\"toc\" role=\"navigation\" aria-labelledby=\"mw-toc-heading\"><input type=\"checkbox\" role=\"button\" id=\"toctogglecheckbox\" class=\"toctogglecheckbox\"
